< Review>
Horrible clinic. I just recently moved from Portland to Los Angeles a few months ago, and promptly got my CA medical card. A little while after I got my CA license and I've since been using my printed paperwork from the DMV along with my US Passport for access to clinics until my license comes in the mail. Today I went into this dispensary and was turned down for the lack of a CA ID, despite having my temporary paperwork from the DMV with my license number (still valid for another two months) and my US Passport. If it's good enough for the cops on the road it should be good enough for you, or do you not understand that temporary paperwork and a passport is valid ID until the laminated card arrives? Either way, I wasn't allowed entry and I sure as hell won't be trying again. There are far better and friendlier dispensaries to go to.< /Review>

< Text>
I have been to La Vera Pizzeria many times because it is the best pizza in Santa Maria. It is owned and operated by a local family who has been around for many years and far surpasses all of the pizza chain restaurants in quality and price. La Vera is the only pizza I get in Santa Maria at this point. My favorite is the combo pizza because they load it with so many toppings! The cheap price does not reflect the quality of the ingredients or the generous servings.

To mix things up, I recently tried a sandwich from there too. This had not been my go-to sandwich place in SM, but after having their pastrami sandwich, I will definitely be going back for more. I never go out of my way to write reviews on the internet, but I was so blown away by this sandwich and their family has been so good to me for so long that I thought this was the least I could do.

Oh and don't forget the buffalo wings! And make sure you get some of their homemade ranch dressing for dipping your pizza, wings, and salads!!< /Text>

<text>As a gadget and electronics geek, it pains me to have to rate Best Buy only three stars, because I used to love this place.  But the fact of the matter is that I easily get identical hardware from online vendors for significantly less money than what Best Buy sells them for.  I used to justify that because Best Buy has their protection plan for hardware - You can get a three year accidental damage warranty for a laptop, for example.  This sounds great, but unfortunately when the time comes to get hardware service on something (in this case a laptop), they mail your equipment away and it's gone for two or three weeks.  I had this happen to a client of mine, and the laptop came back broken - It wouldn't charge or run off of AC power.  So, I went back with them to Best Buy, and the staff said all they could do was send it away for repair again - For another two or three weeks!  The "peace of mind" that their protection plan offers is unfortunately not all that helpful if you need to get your equipment repaired in a timely manner.

All this aside, they still have a great selection of items and you get to physically touch and see what you are getting before you purchase it.  I recognize that this costs more money than a web retailer.  Still, if someone is going to spend several hundred dollars on a premium extended warranty, they really should get premium service, not a month and a half wait to get their hardware back in working order.<//text>< Name>
Jarrod Kailef< /Name>
